[the `unitlessKeys` object shouldn't be emptied (see the `name in unitless` check), as is the case in 4.45.3 and earlier.
`styled-components` uses this to determine wether to add `px` units to CSS like `flex: 1`.](https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10-L12)

### Actual Behaviour

[It removes all properties and this breaks projects that use `styled-components` with `vite`.](https://rollupjs.org/repl/?version=4.46.1&shareable=JTdCJTIyZXhhbXBsZSUyMiUzQW51bGwlMkMlMjJtb2R1bGVzJTIyJTNBJTVCJTdCJTIyY29kZSUyMiUzQSUyMiUyRiUyRiUyMGltcG9ydCUyMHVuaXRsZXNzJTIwZnJvbSUyMCclNDBlbW90aW9uJTJGdW5pdGxlc3MnJTNCJTVDbmltcG9ydCUyMHVuaXRsZXNzJTIwZnJvbSUyMCcuJTJGdW5pdGxlc3MnJTVDbiU1Q24lMkYlMkYlMjBPcmlnaW5hbCUyMGZ1bmN0aW9uJTIwaW4lMjAlNjBzdHlsZWQtY29tcG9uZW50cyU2MCUyQyUyMHN0cmlwcGVkJTIwZm9yJTIwVHlwZVNjcmlwdCUzQSUyMGh0dHBzJTNBJTJGJTJGZ2l0aHViLmNvbSUyRnN0eWxlZC1jb21wb25lbnRzJTJGc3R5bGVkLWNvbXBvbmVudHMlMkZibG9iJTJGZDBiNzNhY2Q5MzFkYWVmOWVlYmI5N2UzNGZlNDU1MmZmYzU3ZDYzZSUyRnBhY2thZ2VzJTJGc3R5bGVkLWNvbXBvbmVudHMlMkZzcmMlMkZ1dGlscyUyRmFkZFVuaXRJZk5lZWRlZC50cyUyM0wxMCU1Q25leHBvcnQlMjBkZWZhdWx0JTIwZnVuY3Rpb24lMjBhZGRVbml0SWZOZWVkZWQobmFtZSUyQyUyMHZhbHVlKSUyMCU3QiU1Q24lMjAlMjAlMkYlMkYlMjBodHRwcyUzQSUyRiUyRmdpdGh1Yi5jb20lMkZhbWlsYWphY2slMkZlc2xpbnQtcGx1Z2luLWZsb3d0eXBlLWVycm9ycyUyRmlzc3VlcyUyRjEzMyU1Q24lMjAlMjBpZiUyMCh2YWx1ZSUyMCUzRCUzRCUyMG51bGwlMjAlN0MlN0MlMjB0eXBlb2YlMjB2YWx1ZSUyMCUzRCUzRCUzRCUyMCdib29sZWFuJyUyMCU3QyU3QyUyMHZhbHVlJTIwJTNEJTNEJTNEJTIwJycpJTIwJTdCJTVDbiUyMCUyMCUyMCUyMHJldHVybiUyMCcnJTNCJTVDbiUyMCUyMCU3RCU1Q24lNUNuJTIwJTIwaWYlMjAodHlwZW9mJTIwdmFsdWUlMjAlM0QlM0QlM0QlMjAnbnVtYmVyJyUyMCUyNiUyNiUyMHZhbHVlJTIwISUzRCUzRCUyMDAlMjAlMjYlMjYlMjAhKG5hbWUlMjBpbiUyMHVuaXRsZXNzKSUyMCUyNiUyNiUyMCFuYW1lLnN0YXJ0c1dpdGgoJy0tJykpJTIwJTdCJTVDbiUyMCUyMCUyMCUyMHJldHVybiUyMCU2MCUyNCU3QnZhbHVlJTdEcHglNjAlM0IlMjAlMkYlMkYlMjBQcmVzdW1lcyUyMGltcGxpY2l0JTIwJ3B4JyUyMHN1ZmZpeCUyMGZvciUyMHVuaXRsZXNzJTIwbnVtYmVycyUyMGV4Y2VwdCUyMGZvciUyMENTUyUyMHZhcmlhYmxlcyU1Q24lMjAlMjAlN0QlNUNuJTVDbiUyMCUyMHJldHVybiUyMFN0cmluZyh2YWx1ZSkudHJpbSgpJTNCJTVDbiU3RCUyMiUyQyUyMmlzRW50cnklMjIlM0F0cnVlJTJDJTIybmFtZSUyMiUzQSUyMm1haW4uanMlMjIlN0QlMkMlN0IlMjJjb2RlJTIyJTNBJTIyJTJGJTJGJTIwRnJvbSUyMGh0dHBzJTNBJTJGJTJGZ2l0aHViLmNvbSUyRmVtb3Rpb24tanMlMkZlbW90aW9uJTJGYmxvYiUyRjQ5MjI5NTUzOTY3YjYwNTBjOTJkOTYwMmViNTc3YmRjNDgxNjdlOTElMkZwYWNrYWdlcyUyRnVuaXRsZXNzJTJGc3JjJTJGaW5kZXgudHMlMjBzdHJpcHBlZCUyMGZyb20lMjBUUyU1Q24     34	        | '!=='

    36	        | '&'
    37	        | '*'

    39	        | '+'

    55	
    56	const binaryOperators: Partial<
    57	        Record<Operator, (left: LiteralValue, right: LiteralValue) => LiteralValueOrUnknown>
    58	> = {
    59	        '!=': (left, right) => left != right,
    60	        '!==': (left, right) => left !== right,
    61	        '%': (left: any, right: any) => left % right,
    62	        '&': (left: any, right: any) => left & right,
    63	        '*': (left: any, right: any) => left * right,
    64	        // At the moment, "**" will be transpiled to Math.pow
    65	        '**': (left: any, right: any) => left ** right,
    66	        '+': (left: any, right: any) => left + right,
    67	        '-': (left: any, right: any) => left - right,
    68	        '/': (left: any, right: any) => left / right,
    69	        '<': (left, right) => left! < right!,
    70	        '<<': (left: any, right: any) => left << right,
    71	        '<=': (left, right) => left! <= right!,
    72	        '==': (left, right) => left == right,
    73	        '===': (left, right) => left === right,
    74	        '>': (left, right) => left! > right!,
    75	        '>=': (left, right) => left! >= right!,
    76	        '>>': (left: any, right: any) => left >> right,
    77	        '>>>': (left: any, right: any) => left >>> right,
    78	        '^': (left: any, right: any) => left ^ right,
    79	        '|': (left: any, right: any) => left | right
    80	        // We use the fallback for cases where we return something unknown
    81	        // in: () => UnknownValue,
    82	        // instanceof: () => UnknownValue,
    83	};
    84	
    85	const UNASSIGNED = Symbol('Unassigned');
    86	
    87	export default class BinaryExpression extends NodeBase implements DeoptimizableEntity {
    88	        declare left: ExpressionNode;
    89	        declare operator: keyof typeof binaryOperators;
    90	        declare right: ExpressionNode;
    91	        declare type: NodeType.tBinaryExpression;
    92	        renderedLiteralValue: string | typeof UnknownValue | typeof UNASSIGNED = UNASSIGNED;
    93	
    94	        deoptimizeCache(): void {
    95	                this.renderedLiteralValue = UnknownValue;
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        getLiteralValueAtPath(
    99	                path: ObjectPath,
   100	                recursionTracker: EntityPathTracker,
   101	                origin: DeoptimizableEntity
   102	        ): LiteralValueOrUnknown {
   103	                if (path.length > 0) return UnknownValue;
   104	                const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   105	                if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   106	
   107	                // Optimize `'export' in namespace`
   108	                if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
   109	                        return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
   110	                }
   111	
   112	                const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   113	                if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   114	
   115	                const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
   116	                if (!operatorFunction) return UnknownValue;
   117	
   118	                return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        getRenderedLiteralValue() {
   122	                // Only optimize `'export' in ns`
   123	                if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
   124	
   125	                if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED) return this.renderedLiteralValue;
   126	                return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(
   127	                        this.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this)
   128	                ));
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        hasEffects(context: HasEffectsContext): boolean {
   132	                // support some implicit type coercion runtime errors
   133	                if (
   134	                        this.operator === '+' &&
   135	                        this.parent instanceof ExpressionStatement &&
   136	                        this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this) === ''
   137	                ) {
   138	                        return true;
   139	                }
   140	                return super.hasEffects(context);
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path: ObjectPath, { type }: NodeInteraction): boolean {
   144	                return type !== INTERACTION_ACCESSED || path.length > 1;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        include(
   148	                context: InclusionContext,
   149	                includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
   150	                _options?: InclusionOptions
   151	        ) {
   152	                this.included = true;
   153	                if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
   154	                        super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
   155	                }
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        includeNode(context: InclusionContext) {
   159	                this.included = true;
   160	                if (this.operator === 'in' && typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
   161	                        this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
   162	                }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        removeAnnotations(code: MagicString) {
   166	                this.left.removeAnnotations(code);
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        render(
   170	                code: MagicString,
   171	                options: RenderOptions,
   172	                { renderedSurroundingElement }: NodeRenderOptions = BLANK
   173	        ): void {
   174	                const renderedLiteralValue = this.getRenderedLiteralValue();
   175	                if (typeof renderedLiteralValue !== 'symbol') {
   176	                        code.overwrite(this.start, this.end, renderedLiteralValue);
   177	                } else {
   178	                        this.left.render(code, options, { renderedSurroundingElement });
   179	                        this.right.render(code, options);
   180	                }
   181	        }
   182	}

    15	import Variable from './Variable';
    16	
    17	export default class NamespaceVariable extends Variable {
    18	        readonly context: AstContext;
    19	        declare isNamespace: true;
    20	        readonly module: Module;
    21	
    22	        private memberVariables: Record<string, Variable> | null = null;
    23	        private mergedNamespaces: readonly Variable[] = [];
    24	        private referencedEarly = false;
    25	        private references: IdentifierBase[] = [];
    26	
    27	        constructor(context: AstContext) {
    28	                super(context.getModuleName());
    29	                this.context = context;
    30	                this.module = context.module;
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        addReference(identifier: IdentifierBase): void {
    34	                this.references.push(identifier);
    35	                this.name = identifier.name;
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        deoptimizeArgumentsOnInteractionAtPath(
    39	                interaction: NodeInteraction,
    40	                path: ObjectPath,
    41	                recursionTracker: EntityPathTracker
    42	        ) {
    43	                if (path.length > 1 || (path.length === 1 && interaction.type === INTERACTION_CALLED)) {
    44	                        const key = path[0];
    45	                        if (typeof key === 'string') {
    46	                                this.getMemberVariables()[key]?.deoptimizeArgumentsOnInteractionAtPath(
    47	                                        interaction,
    48	                                        path.slice(1),
    49	                                        recursionTracker
    50	                                );
    51	                        } else {
    52	                                deoptimizeInteraction(interaction);
    53	                        }
    54	                }
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        deoptimizePath(path: ObjectPath) {
    58	                if (path.length > 1) {
    59	                        const key = path[0];
    60	                        if (typeof key === 'string') {
    61	                                this.getMemberVariables()[key]?.deoptimizePath(path.slice(1));
    62	                        }
    63	                }
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        getLiteralValueAtPath(path: ObjectPath): LiteralValueOrUnknown {
    67	                if (path[0] === SymbolToStringTag) {
    68	                        return 'Module';
    69	                }
    70	                return UnknownValue;
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        getMemberVariables(): Record<string, Variable> {
    74	                if (this.memberVariables) {
    75	                        return this.memberVariables;
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                const memberVariables: Record<string, Variable> = Object.create(null);
    79	                const sortedExports = [...this.context.getExports(), ...this.context.getReexports()].sort();
    80	
    81	                for (const name of sortedExports) {
    82	                        if (name[0] !== '*' && name !== this.module.info.syntheticNamedExports) {
    83	                                const [exportedVariable] = this.context.traceExport(name);
    84	                                if (exportedVariable) {
    85	                                        memberVariables[name] = exportedVariable;
    86	                                }
    87	                        }
    88	                }
    89	                return (this.memberVariables = memberVariables);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(
    93	                path: ObjectPath,
    94	                interaction: NodeInteraction,
    95	                context: HasEffectsContext
    96	        ): boolean {
    97	                const { type } = interaction;
    98	                if (path.length === 0) {
    99	                        // This can only be a call anyway
   100	                        return true;
   101	                }
   102	                if (path.length === 1 && type !== INTERACTION_CALLED) {
   103	                        return type === INTERACTION_ASSIGNED;
   104	                }
   105	                const key = path[0];
   106	                if (typeof key !== 'string') {
   107	                        return true;
   108	                }
   109	                const memberVariable = this.getMemberVariables()[key];
   110	                return (
   111	                        !memberVariable ||
   112	                        memberVariable.hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path.slice(1), interaction, context)
   113	                );
   114	        }

   117	                super.includePath(path, context);

   122	                if (this.mergedNamespaces.length > 0) {
   123	                        this.module.scope.addAccessedGlobals([MERGE_NAMESPACES_VARIABLE], accessedGlobalsByScope);
   124	                }
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        renderBlock(options: RenderOptions): string {
   128	                const {
   129	                        exportNamesByVariable,
   130	                        format,
   131	                        freeze,
   132	                        indent: t,
   133	                        symbols,
   134	                        snippets: { _, cnst, getObject, getPropertyAccess, n, s }
   135	                } = options;
   136	                const memberVariables = this.getMemberVariables();
   137	                const members: [key: string | null, value: string][] = Object.entries(memberVariables)
   138	                        .filter(([_, variable]) => variable.included)
   139	                        .map(([name, variable]) => {
   140	                                if (this.referencedEarly || variable.isReassigned || variable === this) {
   141	                                        return [
   142	                                                null,
   143	                                                `get ${stringifyObjectKeyIfNeeded(name)}${_}()${_}{${_}return ${variable.getName(
   144	                                                        getPropertyAccess
   145	                                                )}${s}${_}}`
   146	                                        ];
   147	                                }
   148	
   149	                                return [name, variable.getName(getPropertyAccess)];
   150	                        });
   151	                members.unshift([null, `__proto__:${_}null`]);
   152	
   153	                let output = getObject(members, { lineBreakIndent: { base: '', t } });
   154	                if (this.mergedNamespaces.length > 0) {
   155	                        const assignmentArguments = this.mergedNamespaces.map(variable =>
   156	                                variable.getName(getPropertyAccess)
   157	                        );
   158	                        output = `/*#__PURE__*/${MERGE_NAMESPACES_VARIABLE}(${output},${_}[${assignmentArguments.join(
   159	                                `,${_}`
   160	                        )}])`;
   161	                } else {
   162	                        // The helper to merge namespaces will also take care of freezing and toStringTag

2025-12-27 00:14:49,554 - INFO - swea-agent-rollup__rollup-6041 - 💭 THOUGHT
Aha! Now I can see the issue. Both `NamespaceVariable` and `ExternalVariable` can have `isNamespace` set to `true`. The problem is:

1. In `BinaryExpression.ts` line 108, the code checks `this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable`
2. But for external modules (like `import unitless from './unitless'`), the variable is an `ExternalVariable` with `isNamespace: true`, not a `NamespaceVariable`
3. So the optimization tries to call `this.right.variable.context.traceExport()` on an `ExternalVariable`, which doesn't have a `context` property, causing incorrect behavior

The fix should check if the variable is an internal namespace (NamespaceVariable) and not an external namespace (ExternalVariable with isNamespace=true).

Let me look at the test case first to understand the expected behavior:

const mainCode = `// import unitless from '"'"'@emotion/unitless'"'"';
import unitless from '"'"'./unitless'"'"'

// Original function in \`styled-components\`, stripped for TypeScript: https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10
export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  // https://github.com/amilajack/eslint-plugin-flowtype-errors/issues/133
  if (value == null || typeof value === '"'"'boolean'"'"' || value === '"'"''"'"') {
    return '"'"''"'"';
  }

  if (typeof value === '"'"'number'"'"' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless) && !name.startsWith('"'"'--'"'"')) {
    return \`\${value}px\`; // Presumes implicit '"'"'px'"'"' suffix for unitless numbers except for CSS variables
  }

  return String(value).trim();
}`;

async function test() {
  try {
    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
      input: '"'"'main.js'"'"',
      plugins: [{
        name: '"'"'test-plugin'"'"',
        resolveId(source) {
          if (source === '"'"'main.js'"'"') return '"'"'main.js'"'"';
          if (source === '"'"'./unitless'"'"') return '"'"'unitless.js'"'"';
          return null;
        },
        load(id) {
          if (id === '"'"'main.js'"'"') return mainCode;
          if (id === '"'"'unitless.js'"'"') return unitlessCode;
          return null;
        }
      }]
    });

    const { output } = await bundle.generate({
      format: '"'"'esm'"'"'
    });

    const result = output[0].code;
    console.log('"'"'Generated code:'"'"');
    console.log(result);
    console.log('"'"'\n---\n'"'"');

    // Check if unitless object is empty
    if (result.includes('"'"'unitlessKeys = {};'"'"') || result.includes('"'"'unitlessKeys = {}'"'"')) {
      console.error('"'"'❌ FAIL: unitlessKeys object was incorrectly optimized away!'"'"');
      console.error('"'"'The object should contain all the properties, not be empty.'"'"');
      return false;
    } else if (result.includes('"'"'animationIterationCount'"'"') && result.includes('"'"'flexGrow'"'"')) {
      console.log('"'"'✅ PASS: unitlessKeys object is preserved correctly.'"'"');
      return true;
    } else {
      console.error('"'"'❌ FAIL: unitlessKeys object is missing expected properties.'"'"');
      return false;
    }

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('"'"'Error during test:'"'"', error);
    return false;
  }
}

test().then(success => {
  process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
});

let unitlessKeys = {
  };

// import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';

// Original function in `styled-components`, stripped for TypeScript: https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10
function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  // https://github.com/amilajack/eslint-plugin-flowtype-errors/issues/133
  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
    return `${value}px`; // Presumes implicit 'px' suffix for unitless numbers except for CSS variables
  }

  return String(value).trim();
}

export { addUnitIfNeeded as default };

Looking at the code, I can see that:

1. Line 108-109: `getLiteralValueAtPath` tries to optimize `'export' in namespace` by checking if `this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable`, and if so, calls `this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null`
2. Line 123: `getRenderedLiteralValue` checks `!this.right.variable?.isNamespace` before trying to optimize

The problem is that for an imported namespace from another module (like `import unitless from './unitless'`), the variable is an `ExternalVariable` with `isNamespace: true`. When we try to check if properties exist in this external namespace:
- Line 108 checks `instanceof NamespaceVariable`, which is `false` for ExternalVariable
- But Line 123 checks `isNamespace`, which is `true` for both NamespaceVariable AND ExternalVariable

So for ExternalVariable, the code at line 108-109 returns `UnknownValue` (since the instanceof check fails), but then line 126-128 still tries to get the literal value and render it. Since ExternalVariable doesn't have a `context` property, the optimization doesn't work correctly.

Wait, let me re-read the code more carefully. Looking at line 123:

```typescript
if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
```

This says: if it's not an 'in' operator, OR if the right side is NOT a namespace, return UnknownValue.

So it only tries to optimize when:
1. operator is 'in'
2. right side variable is a namespace (isNamespace is true)

But then on line 108, it only actually performs the optimization if it's a NamespaceVariable. For ExternalVariable, it falls through to the normal binary operator handling.

The issue is that when the variable is an ExternalVariable with isNamespace=true:
1. Line 123 passes (because isNamespace is true)
2. Line 126-128 calls getLiteralValueAtPath
3. Line 108 instanceof check fails (it's not a NamespaceVariable)
4. Falls through to line 112-118 which tries to evaluate the binary expression normally
5. Since it can't know the properties of an external module at build time, it should return UnknownValue

let unitlessKeys = {
  };

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
    return value + 'px';
  }

  return String(value).trim();
}

export { addUnitIfNeeded as default };

   598	function resolveNamespaceVariables(
   599	        baseVariable: Variable,
   600	        path: PathWithPositions,
   601	        astContext: AstContext
   602	): Variable | 'undefined' | null {
   603	        if (path.length === 0) return baseVariable;
   604	        if (!baseVariable.isNamespace || baseVariable instanceof ExternalVariable) return null;

Now I see the issue! 

Line 123 checks: `if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;`

This means it allows optimization for BOTH NamespaceVariable AND ExternalVariable (since both have `isNamespace` set to true).

But line 108 only handles NamespaceVariable: `if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable)`

So for ExternalVariable:
1. Line 123 passes (because ExternalVariable.isNamespace is true)
2. Line 126-128 calls getLiteralValueAtPath
3. Line 108 instanceof check fails (it's not a NamespaceVariable)
4. Falls through to line 112-118
5. Since we're checking if a string is in an object, and the object is an imported namespace, line 112 should return UnknownValue for the right side

But wait, let me check what getLiteralValueAtPath returns for a namespace variable:

import { UnknownValue } from '../nodes/shared/Expression';

export function getRenderedLiteralValue(value: unknown) {
	if (value === undefined) {
		return 'void 0';
	}
	if (typeof value === 'boolean') {
		return String(value);
	}
	if (typeof value === 'string') {
		return JSON.stringify(value);
	}
	if (typeof value === 'number') {
		return getSimplifiedNumber(value);
	}
	return UnknownValue;
}

function getSimplifiedNumber(value: number) {
	if (Object.is(-0, value)) {
		return '-0';
	}
	const exp = value.toExponential();
	const [base, exponent] = exp.split('e');
	const floatLength = base.split('.')[1]?.length || 0;
	const finalizedExp = `${base.replace('.', '')}e${parseInt(exponent) - floatLength}`;
	const stringifiedValue = String(value).replace('+', '');
	return finalizedExp.length < stringifiedValue.length ? finalizedExp : stringifiedValue;
}

	includePath(path: ObjectPath, context: InclusionContext): void;

	/**
	 * Special version of include for assignment left-hand sides which ensures
	 * that accessors are handled correctly. This is necessary to do from the
	 * child so that member expressions can use the correct this value.
	 * setAssignedValue needs to be called during initialise to use this.
	 */

		context: InclusionContext,

   213	        includePath(path: ObjectPath, context: InclusionContext): void {
   214	                if (!this.includedPathTracker.includePathAndGetIfIncluded(path)) {
   215	                        this.module.scope.context.requestTreeshakingPass();
   216	                        if (!this.included) {
   217	                                // This will reduce the number of tree-shaking passes by eagerly
   218	                                // including inits. By pushing this here instead of directly including
   219	                                // we avoid deep call stacks.
   220	                                this.module.scope.context.newlyIncludedVariableInits.add(this.init);
   221	                        }
   222	                        super.includePath(path, context);
   223	                        for (const declaration of this.declarations) {
   224	                                // If node is a default export, it can save a tree-shaking run to include the full declaration now
   225	                                if (!declaration.included) declaration.include(context, false);
   226	                                let node = declaration.parent as Node;
   227	                                while (!node.included) {
   228	                                        // We do not want to properly include parents in case they are part of a dead branch
   229	                                        // in which case .include() might pull in more dead code
   230	                                        node.includeNode(context);
   231	                                        if (node.type === NodeType.Program) break;
   232	                                        node = node.parent as Node;
   233	                                }
   234	                                /**
   235	                                 * import('foo').then(m => {
   236	                                 *   console.log(m.foo)
   237	                                 * })
   238	                                 */
   239	                                if (
   240	                                        this.kind === 'parameter' &&
   241	                                        (isArrowFunctionExpressionNode(declaration.parent) ||
   242	                                                isFunctionExpressionNode(declaration.parent)) &&
   243	                                        isCallExpressionNode(declaration.parent.parent) &&
   244	                                        isMemberExpressionNode(declaration.parent.parent.callee) &&
   245	                                        isIdentifierNode(declaration.parent.parent.callee.property) &&
   246	                                        declaration.parent.parent.callee.property.name === 'then' &&
   247	                                        isImportExpressionNode(declaration.parent.parent.callee.object)
   248	                                ) {
   249	                                        declaration.parent.parent.callee.object.includePath(path);

   255	                                this.additionalInitializers?.forEach(initializer =>

OK, so at line 254, when the path is UNKNOWN_PATH (which has length > 0), it calls `this.init.includePath(limitConcatenatedPathDepth(this.initPath, path), context)`.

`this.init` is the initializer of the variable, which in our case is the Identifier that references `unitlessKeys` from the imported module.

But wait... in our case, `unitless` is imported via `import unitless from './unitless'`. So the init would be the import statement, not the actual object literal.

Let me think about this differently. The issue is that when we have `!(name in unitless)` where `name` is a variable:

1. The BinaryExpression `name in unitless` cannot be optimized because `name` is not a constant
2. So getRenderedLiteralValue returns UnknownValue
3. BinaryExpression.includeNode calls `this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context)`
4. `this.right` is an Identifier referencing the imported `unitless` variable
5. This should include the entire `unitless` object with all its properties

But somehow the properties are being removed. Let me check if there's an issue with how the optimization in BinaryExpression getRenderedLiteralValue is checking for ExternalVariable.

Wait! I just realized the actual problem. Look at line 123 in BinaryExpression.ts:

```typescript
if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
```

This checks `!this.right.variable?.isNamespace`. If the variable is NOT a namespace, it returns UnknownValue (meaning no optimization).

BUT, for a default import like `import unitless from './unitless'`, the variable is NOT a namespace! It's just a regular variable that references the default export.

Only namespace imports like `import * as unitless from './unitless'` have `isNamespace = true`.

So for a default import, line 123 returns UnknownValue immediately, which means no optimization should happen. But somehow it's still happening!

Let me test this theory:

🎬 ACTION

const unitlessCode = `
let unitlessKeys = {
  flex: 1,
  flexGrow: 1
}
export { unitlessKeys }`;

const mainCode = `

Wait, I think I see the issue now! Look at the logic:

Line 123 checks: `if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;`

This should prevent optimization for non-namespace variables. But the problem is that in our test case with `import * as ns from './unitless'` and then `const unitless = ns.unitlessKeys`, the variable `unitless` is a LocalVariable, not a namespace variable!

So line 123 should return UnknownValue, which means no optimization. But somehow the properties are still being removed.

Let me check if there's tree-shaking happening at a different level. Maybe the issue is with ObjectExpression tree-shaking.

2025-12-27 00:26:51,553 - INFO - swea-agent-rollup__rollup-6041 - 💭 THOUGHT
So UnknownKey is a symbol. So `typeof UnknownKey === 'string'` is false, which means line 381 in ObjectEntity.ts should be triggered, including all properties.

But somehow it's not working. Let me check if there's an issue with how the path is being passed from BinaryExpression to the Identifier to the ObjectExpression.

Wait, let me re-read the BinaryExpression.includeNode code:

```typescript
includeNode(context: InclusionContext) {
    this.included = true;
    if (this.operator === 'in' && typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
        this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
    }
}
```

So it calls `this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context)`. `this.right` is an Identifier. And we saw that IdentifierBase.includePath calls `includeVariableInModule`, which calls `includeVariable`, which calls `variable.includePath(path, context)`.

For a LocalVariable with an object initializer, this should eventually call ObjectExpression.includePath with UNKNOWN_PATH.

But wait, maybe the issue is that `includeNode` is not being called! Let me check when includeNode is called on BinaryExpression.

Looking at the NodeBase and ExpressionEntity, includePath calls includeNode if not already included. But for BinaryExpression, maybe there's a different flow?

Actually, I just noticed something important. In BinaryExpression, line 147-156 is the `include` method:

```typescript
include(
    context: InclusionContext,
    includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
    _options?: InclusionOptions
) {
    this.included = true;
    if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
        super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
    }
}
```

So if the literal value can't be determined (returns a symbol), it calls super.include which should include both left and right children.

But line 158-163 is `includeNode`:

```typescript
includeNode(context: InclusionContext) {
    this.included = true;
    if (this.operator === 'in' && typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
        this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
    }
}
```

This is a special optimization for the `in` operator - it includes the right side with UNKNOWN_PATH.

Now let me check when `includeNode` is called. Looking at ExpressionEntity.includePath (line 117-119 in Expression.ts):

```typescript
includePath(_path: ObjectPath, context: InclusionContext): void {
    if (!this.included) this.includeNode(context);
}
```

So `includeNode` is called when `includePath` is called and the node is not yet included.

But `BinaryExpression.include` is called first (not `includePath`), which sets `this.included = true`. So when `includePath` is later called, `includeNode` is NOT called because `this.included` is already true!

Let me verify this theory. The flow might be:
1. UnaryExpression (the `!`) includes its argument (the Binary Expression)
2. UnaryExpression.include calls argument.include
3. BinaryExpression.include sets included = true and calls super.include if it can't optimize
4. super.include includes left and right children normally
5. Later, if something calls BinaryExpression.includePath, the check `if (!this.included)` is false, so includeNode is NOT called
6. So `this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context)` is NEVER called!

That's the bug! The `includeNode` method with the special UNKNOWN_PATH logic is never called if `include` is called first.

Now let me check if this is actually what happens. Let me look for where `include` is called on the BinaryExpression:

Looking at UnaryExpression.include (lines 111-129 in UnaryExpression.ts):

```typescript
include(
    context: InclusionContext,
    includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
    _options?: InclusionOptions
): void {
    if (!this.deoptimized) this.applyDeoptimizations();
    this.included = true;
    // Check if the argument is an identifier that should be preserved as a reference for readability
    const shouldPreserveArgument =
        this.argument instanceof Identifier && this.argument.variable?.included;
    if (
        typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue(includeChildrenRecursively) === 'symbol' ||
        this.argument.shouldBeIncluded(context) ||
        shouldPreserveArgument
    ) {
        this.argument.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively);
        this.renderedLiteralValue = UnknownValue;
    }
}
```

Line 126: `this.argument.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively)` - Yes! It calls `include`, not `includePath`!

So that's the bug. When a BinaryExpression with `in` operator is included via `include()`, the special UNKNOWN_PATH logic in `includeNode()` is never executed.

The fix should be to move the UNKNOWN_PATH logic from `includeNode` to `include`, or to ensure `includeNode` is always called even when `include` is called first.

Let me check the fix that was added in commit 6031a33ea:

Looking at the diff again:
```diff
-		if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable?.isNamespace) {
-			return (
-				(this.right.variable as NamespaceVariable).context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null
-			);
+		if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
+			return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
```

This change was to prevent the optimization from applying to ExternalVariable namespaces. But the real issue is that the `includeNode` method with the UNKNOWN_PATH logic is not being called!

Let me look at how to fix this. The solution is to also add the UNKNOWN_PATH logic to the `include` method. Let me check how this should be done:

		includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,

		context: InclusionContext,
		includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
		_options?: InclusionOptions

		this.included = true;
		if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
			super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);

	include(
		context: InclusionContext,
		includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
		_options?: InclusionOptions
	) {
		this.included = true;
		if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
			super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
		}
	}

	includeNode(context: InclusionContext) {
		this.included = true;
		if (this.operator === 'in' && typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
			this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
		}
	}

	removeAnnotations(code: MagicString) {
		this.left.removeAnnotations(code);
	}

	render(
		code: MagicString,
		options: RenderOptions,
		{ renderedSurroundingElement }: NodeRenderOptions = BLANK
	): void {
		const renderedLiteralValue = this.getRenderedLiteralValue();
		if (typeof renderedLiteralValue !== 'symbol') {
			code.overwrite(this.start, this.end, renderedLiteralValue);
		} else {
			this.left.render(code, options, { renderedSurroundingElement });
			this.right.render(code, options);
		}
	}
}

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+
+with open('/testbed/src/ast/nodes/BinaryExpression.ts', 'r') as f:
+    lines = f.readlines()
+
+# Find the include method (around line 147-156)
+in_include_method = False
+brace_count = 0
+start_line = None
+end_line = None
+
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    if 'include(' in line and 'context: InclusionContext' in lines[i+1]:
+        in_include_method = True
+        start_line = i
+        brace_count = 0
+        continue
+    
+    if in_include_method:
+        for char in line:
+            if char == '{':
+                brace_count += 1
+            elif char == '}':
+                brace_count -= 1
+        
+        if brace_count < 0:  # Found closing brace
+            end_line = i
+            break
+
+if start_line is None or end_line is None:
+    print("Could not find the include method!")
+    exit(1)
+
+# Extract the existing method
+original = ''.join(lines[start_line:end_line+1])
+print(f"Found include method at lines {start_line+1} to {end_line+1}")
+print(f"Original method:\n{original}")
+
+# Create the new version with the fix
+# We need to add the code before the final closing brace
+lines_to_add = [
+    '\t\t\t// For the \'in\' operator with unknown value, we need to include the right side with UNKNOWN_PATH\n',
+    '\t\t\t// to ensure all properties are preserved\n',
+    '\t\t\tif (this.operator === \'in\') {\n',
+    '\t\t\t\tthis.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);\n',
+    '\t\t\t}\n',
+]
+
+# Find the line with the second closing brace (end of the if statement)
+insert_pos = None
+for i in range(start_line, end_line+1):
+    if '\t\t}' in lines[i] and 'super.include' in ''.join(lines[max(0,i-3):i]):
+        insert_pos = i + 1
+        break
+
+if insert_pos:
+    print(f"Inserting fix at line {insert_pos+1}")
+    lines[insert_pos:insert_pos] = lines_to_add
+    
+    with open('/testbed/src/ast/nodes/BinaryExpression.ts', 'w') as f:
+        f.writelines(lines)
+    
+    print("Successfully patched BinaryExpression.ts!")
+else:
+    print("Could not find insertion point!")

+import type MagicString from 'magic-string';
+import { BLANK } from '../../utils/blank';
+import type { NodeRenderOptions, RenderOptions } from '../../utils/renderHelpers';
+import type { DeoptimizableEntity } from '../DeoptimizableEntity';
+import type { HasEffectsContext, InclusionContext } from '../ExecutionContext';
+import type { NodeInteraction } from '../NodeInteractions';
+import { INTERACTION_ACCESSED } from '../NodeInteractions';
+import {
+	EMPTY_PATH,
+	type EntityPathTracker,
+	type ObjectPath,
+	SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER,
+	UNKNOWN_PATH
+} from '../utils/PathTracker';
+import { getRenderedLiteralValue } from '../utils/renderLiteralValue';
+import NamespaceVariable from '../variables/NamespaceVariable';
+import ExpressionStatement from './ExpressionStatement';
+import type { LiteralValue } from './Literal';
+import type * as NodeType from './NodeType';
+import {
+	type InclusionOptions,
+	type LiteralValueOrUnknown,
+	UnknownValue
+} from './shared/Expression';
+import {
+	doNotDeoptimize,
+	type ExpressionNode,
+	type IncludeChildren,
+	NodeBase
+} from './shared/Node';
+
+type Operator =
+	| '!='
+	| '!=='
+	| '%'
+	| '&'
+	| '*'
+	| '**'
+	| '+'
+	| '-'
+	| '/'
+	| '<'
+	| '<<'
+	| '<='
+	| '=='
+	| '==='
+	| '>'
+	| '>='
+	| '>>'
+	| '>>>'
+	| '^'
+	| '|'
+	| 'in'
+	| 'instanceof';
+
+const binaryOperators: Partial<
+	Record<Operator, (left: LiteralValue, right: LiteralValue) => LiteralValueOrUnknown>
+> = {
+	'!=': (left, right) => left != right,
+	'!==': (left, right) => left !== right,
+	'%': (left: any, right: any) => left % right,
+	'&': (left: any, right: any) => left & right,
+	'*': (left: any, right: any) => left * right,
+	// At the moment, "**" will be transpiled to Math.pow
+	'**': (left: any, right: any) => left ** right,
+	'+': (left: any, right: any) => left + right,
+	'-': (left: any, right: any) => left - right,
+	'/': (left: any, right: any) => left / right,
+	'<': (left, right) => left! < right!,
+	'<<': (left: any, right: any) => left << right,
+	'<=': (left, right) => left! <= right!,
+	'==': (left, right) => left == right,
+	'===': (left, right) => left === right,
+	'>': (left, right) => left! > right!,
+	'>=': (left, right) => left! >= right!,
+	'>>': (left: any, right: any) => left >> right,
+	'>>>': (left: any, right: any) => left >>> right,
+	'^': (left: any, right: any) => left ^ right,
+	'|': (left: any, right: any) => left | right
+	// We use the fallback for cases where we return something unknown
+	// in: () => UnknownValue,
+	// instanceof: () => UnknownValue,
+};
+
+const UNASSIGNED = Symbol('Unassigned');
+
+export default class BinaryExpression extends NodeBase implements DeoptimizableEntity {
+	declare left: ExpressionNode;
+	declare operator: keyof typeof binaryOperators;
+	declare right: ExpressionNode;
+	declare type: NodeType.tBinaryExpression;
+	renderedLiteralValue: string | typeof UnknownValue | typeof UNASSIGNED = UNASSIGNED;
+
+	deoptimizeCache(): void {
+		this.renderedLiteralValue = UnknownValue;
+	}
+
+	getLiteralValueAtPath(
+		path: ObjectPath,
+		recursionTracker: EntityPathTracker,
+		origin: DeoptimizableEntity
+	): LiteralValueOrUnknown {
+		if (path.length > 0) return UnknownValue;
+		const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
+		if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
+
+		// Optimize `'export' in namespace`
+		if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
+			return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
+		}
+
+		const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
+		if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
+
+		const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
+		if (!operatorFunction) return UnknownValue;
+
+		return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
+	}
+
+	getRenderedLiteralValue() {
+		// Only optimize `'export' in ns`
+		if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
+
+		if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED) return this.renderedLiteralValue;
+		return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(
+			this.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this)
+		));
+	}
+
+	hasEffects(context: HasEffectsContext): boolean {
+		// support some implicit type coercion runtime errors
+		if (
+			this.operator === '+' &&
+			this.parent instanceof ExpressionStatement &&
+			this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this) === ''
+		) {
+			return true;
+		}
+		return super.hasEffects(context);
+	}
+
+	hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path: ObjectPath, { type }: NodeInteraction): boolean {
+		return type !== INTERACTION_ACCESSED || path.length > 1;
+	}
+
+	include(
+		context: InclusionContext,
+		includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
+		_options?: InclusionOptions
+	) {
+		this.included = true;
+		if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
+			super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
+		}
+	}
+
+	includeNode(context: InclusionContext) {
+		this.included = true;
+		if (this.operator === 'in' && typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
+			this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
+		}
+	}
+
+	removeAnnotations(code: MagicString) {
+		this.left.removeAnnotations(code);
+	}
+
+	render(
+		code: MagicString,
+		options: RenderOptions,
+		{ renderedSurroundingElement }: NodeRenderOptions = BLANK
+	): void {
+		const renderedLiteralValue = this.getRenderedLiteralValue();
+		if (typeof renderedLiteralValue !== 'symbol') {
+			code.overwrite(this.start, this.end, renderedLiteralValue);
+		} else {
+			this.left.render(code, options, { renderedSurroundingElement });
+			this.right.render(code, options);
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+BinaryExpression.prototype.applyDeoptimizations = doNotDeoptimize;

+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');
+
+const unitlessCode = `
+let unitlessKeys = {
+  flex: 1,
+  flexGrow: 1
+}
+export default unitlessKeys`;
+
+const mainCode = `
+import unitless from './unitless'
+console.log(typeof unitless);
+console.log('flex' in unitless);
+`;
+
+(async () => {
+  const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
+    input: 'main.js',
+    plugins: [{
+      name: 'test',
+      resolveId(source) {
+        if (source === 'main.js') return 'main.js';
+        if (source === './unitless') return 'unitless.js';
+        return null;
+      },
+      load(id) {
+        if (id === 'main.js') return mainCode;
+        if (id === 'unitless.js') return unitlessCode;
+        return null;
+      }
+    }]
+  });
+
+  const { output } = await bundle.generate({ format: 'esm' });
+  console.log(output[0].code);
+})();

+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');

+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');
+
+const unitlessCode = `
+export let unitlessKeys = {
+  flex: 1,
+  flexGrow: 1,
+  opacity: 1
+}`;
+
+const mainCode = `
+import { unitlessKeys } from './unitless'
+export function check(name, value) {
+  console.log('checking', name);
+  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys)) {

+// Test case to reproduce the styled-components issue
+const fs = require('fs');
+const path = require('path');
+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup.js');
+
+const unitlessCode = `// From https://github.com/emotion-js/emotion/blob/49229553967b6050c92d9602eb577bdc48167e91/packages/unitless/src/index.ts stripped from TS
+
+let unitlessKeys = {
+  animationIterationCount: 1,
+  aspectRatio: 1,
+  borderImageOutset: 1,
+  borderImageSlice: 1,
+  borderImageWidth: 1,
+  boxFlex: 1,
+  boxFlexGroup: 1,
+  boxOrdinalGroup: 1,
+  columnCount: 1,
+  columns: 1,
+  flex: 1,
+  flexGrow: 1,
+  flexPositive: 1,
+  flexShrink: 1,
+  flexNegative: 1,
+  flexOrder: 1,
+  gridRow: 1,
+  gridRowEnd: 1,
+  gridRowSpan: 1,
+  gridRowStart: 1,
+  gridColumn: 1,
+  gridColumnEnd: 1,
+  gridColumnSpan: 1,
+  gridColumnStart: 1,
+  msGridRow: 1,
+  msGridRowSpan: 1,
+  msGridColumn: 1,
+  msGridColumnSpan: 1,
+  fontWeight: 1,
+  lineHeight: 1,
+  opacity: 1,
+  order: 1,
+  orphans: 1,
+  scale: 1,
+  tabSize: 1,
+  widows: 1,
+  zIndex: 1,
+  zoom: 1,
+  WebkitLineClamp: 1,
+
+  // SVG-related properties
+  fillOpacity: 1,
+  floodOpacity: 1,
+  stopOpacity: 1,
+  strokeDasharray: 1,
+  strokeDashoffset: 1,
+  strokeMiterlimit: 1,
+  strokeOpacity: 1,
+  strokeWidth: 1
+}
+
+export default unitlessKeys`;
+
+const mainCode = `// import unitless from '@emotion/unitless';
+import unitless from './unitless'
+
+// Original function in \`styled-components\`, stripped for TypeScript: https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10
+export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
+  // https://github.com/amilajack/eslint-plugin-flowtype-errors/issues/133
+  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
+    return '';
+  }
+
+  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
+    return \`\${value}px\`; // Presumes implicit 'px' suffix for unitless numbers except for CSS variables
+  }
+
+  return String(value).trim();
+}`;
+
+async function test() {
+  try {
+    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
+      input: 'main.js',
+      plugins: [{
+        name: 'test-plugin',
+        resolveId(source) {
+          if (source === 'main.js') return 'main.js';
+          if (source === './unitless') return 'unitless.js';
+          return null;
+        },
+        load(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return mainCode;
+          if (id === 'unitless.js') return unitlessCode;
+          return null;
+        }
+      }]
+    });
+
+    const { output } = await bundle.generate({
+      format: 'esm'
+    });
+
+    const result = output[0].code;
+    console.log('Generated code:');
+    console.log(result);
+    console.log('\n---\n');
+
+    // Check if unitless object is empty
+    if (result.includes('unitlessKeys = {};') || result.includes('unitlessKeys = {}')) {
+      console.error('❌ FAIL: unitlessKeys object was incorrectly optimized away!');
+      console.error('The object should contain all the properties, not be empty.');
+      return false;
+    } else if (result.includes('animationIterationCount') && result.includes('flexGrow')) {
+      console.log('✅ PASS: unitlessKeys object is preserved correctly.');
+      return true;
+    } else {
+      console.error('❌ FAIL: unitlessKeys object is missing expected properties.');
+      return false;
+    }
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error during test:', error);
+    return false;
+  }
+}
+
+test().then(success => {
+  process.exit(success ? 0 : 1);
+});
